<div id="review_1779594775" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1779594775" />
    <a title="Vaso" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15818014-vaso"><img alt="Vaso" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1395921377p2/15818014.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1779594775?book_show_action=true">Nov 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vaso" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vaso" href="/user/show/15818014-vaso">Vaso</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/6562918-lightning">review of another edition</a>


          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Vaso by: </span>
      <a href="/user/show/4929702-christina">Christina</a>
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15818014-vaso?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1779594775" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15113260234823777971">The story begins in the '70s and we see a man visiting Laura's life from the day she was born. Sometimes, he interferes and helps her avoid tough situations. He vanishes for many years and when he appears again, they are involved in a gunfire and her husband dies. The story is well developed, with as much drama as needed.<br/>It is the first book I read from this author and a good friend of mine, was rather surprised that I missed it. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1623553761" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1623553761" />
    <a title="Stephen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4809022-stephen"><img alt="Stephen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1295019472p2/4809022.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1623553761?book_show_action=true">Apr 28, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Stephen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Stephen" href="/user/show/4809022-stephen">Stephen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781472230287" href="/book/show/24517369-lightning">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1623553761" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16830967020386073403">Usually really enjoy time travel books (<a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10644930.11_22_63' title='11/22/63 by Stephen King' rel='nofollow noopener'>11/22/63</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40526.Time_and_Again__Time___1_' title='Time and Again (Time, #1) by Jack Finney' rel='nofollow noopener'>Time and Again</a> being two of my favourites) but this back to front time travel book (without giving the story away - people from the past appearing in the present) was just silly and completely unbelievable throughout. Trying too hard to be like a Stephen King book but was just a pale imitation and really dragged for me, so much so that I was tempted to give up at times. Seems like I am in a minority based on the ratings but don't think I'll be</span>
  <span id="freeText16830967020386073403" style="display:none">Usually really enjoy time travel books (<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/10644930.11_22_63" title="11/22/63 by Stephen King" rel="nofollow noopener">11/22/63</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/40526.Time_and_Again__Time___1_" title="Time and Again (Time, #1) by Jack Finney" rel="nofollow noopener">Time and Again</a> being two of my favourites) but this back to front time travel book (without giving the story away - people from the past appearing in the present) was just silly and completely unbelievable throughout. Trying too hard to be like a Stephen King book but was just a pale imitation and really dragged for me, so much so that I was tempted to give up at times. Seems like I am in a minority based on the ratings but don't think I'll be trying anymore Dean Koontz books which will maybe save me lots of time and money given how many there are !</span>
  <a data-text-id="16830967020386073403" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('J651VSv4YQ6VmrRvPp8iv1D8Fyk1CsRNpoaiW9EypVwdiByHkKaoZjKxAA7JaihghqPw4fuHSir9+OTqHHFXxg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IC8V4OKFcetwILFAkoFtixnyh4uj/KOiyblZfCe0m+YaCXwyWdu4g9cLBSFldGdUz61gQ21xLcWSxx/N6vdpfA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
